Senate File 2204 - Reprinted


                                 SENATE FILE 

                                 SENATE FILE 
                                 SENATE FILE                                  SENATE FILE                                  BY  COMMITTEE ON COMMERCE

                                 (SUCCESSOR TO SF 2019)
       (As Amended and Passed by the Senate March 8, 2016)

 A BILL FOR

  1 An Act relating to insurance coverage for the assessment and
  2    treatment of eating disorders and including applicability
  3    date provisions.
  4 BE IT ENACTED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    SF 2204 (2) 86
    av/rj/jh

PAG LIN

                                 (SUCCESSOR TO SF 2019)

  1  1    Section 1.    4 BE IT ENACTED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:

PAG LIN



  1  1    Section 1.      SF 2204 (2) 86
    av/rj/jh

PAG LIN



  1  1    Section 1.      av/rj/jh

PAG LIN



  1  1    Section 1.  

  1  1    Section 1.  
  1  1    Section 1.    1  1    Section 1.    1  2 coverage.
  1  3    1.  Notwithstanding the uniformity of treatment requirements
  1  4 of section 514C.6, a policy, contract, or plan providing for
  1  5 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  1  6 shall provide coverage benefits for the diagnostic assessment
  1  7 and treatment of eating disorders.
  1  8    2.  As used in this section, unless the context otherwise
  1  9 requires:
  1 10    a.  "Diagnostic assessment of eating disorders" means
  1 11 medically necessary assessments, evaluations, or tests
  1 12 performed by a physician or psychiatrist licensed pursuant to
  1 13 chapter 148, a psychologist licensed pursuant to chapter 154B,
  1 14 an advanced registered nurse practitioner licensed pursuant to
  1 15 chapter 152 or 152E, a dietician licensed pursuant to chapter
  1 16 152A, a social worker licensed pursuant to chapter 154C, or
  1 17 a mental health counselor or marital and family therapist
  1 18 licensed pursuant to chapter 154D, to diagnose whether an
  1 19 individual has an eating disorder.
  1 20    b.  "Eating disorders" means pica, rumination disorder,
  1 21 avoidant or restrictive food intake disorder, anorexia nervosa,
  1 22 bulimia nervosa, binge eating disorder, other specified feeding
  1 23 or eating disorder, or any other eating disorder not otherwise
  1 24 specified.  The commissioner, by rule, shall define "eating
  1 25 disorders" consistent with definitions provided in the most
  1 26 recent edition of the American psychiatric association's
  1 27 diagnostic and statistical manual of mental disorders, as such
  1 28 definitions may be amended from time to time. The commissioner
  1 29 may adopt the definitions provided in such manual by reference.
  1 30    c.  "Pharmacy care" means medications prescribed by
  1 31 a licensed physician or psychiatrist and includes any
  1 32 health=related services deemed medically necessary to determine
  1 33 the need for or effectiveness of the medications prescribed,
  1 34 but only to the extent that coverage of such medications is
  1 35 included in the insured's health coverage benefits.
  2  1    d.  "Psychiatric care" or "psychological care" means
  2  2 direct or consultative services provided during inpatient
  2  3 hospitalization, partial hospitalization, residential
  2  4 care, intensive outpatient treatment, follow=up outpatient
  2  5 care, or counseling, provided by a licensed psychiatrist or
  2  6 psychologist.
  2  7    e.  "Therapeutic care" means medical care or behavioral
  2  8 interventions provided by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2  9 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 10 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 11 and family therapist.
  2 12    f.  "Treatment of eating disorders" means treatment that
  2 13 is identified in a treatment plan and includes medically
  2 14 necessary pharmacy care, psychiatric or psychological
  2 15 care, or therapeutic care, that is provided by a licensed
  2 16 physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced registered
  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:
  4 11    a.  Individual or group accident and sickness insurance
  4 12 providing coverage on an expense=incurred basis.
  4 13    b.  An individual or group hospital or medical service
  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.
       SF 2204 (2) 86
       av/rj/jh

  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:
  4 11    a.  Individual or group accident and sickness insurance
  4 12 providing coverage on an expense=incurred basis.
  4 13    b.  An individual or group hospital or medical service
  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.

  4 21 employees.

  4 23 public health.

  1  6 shall provide coverage benefits for the diagnostic assessment
  1  7 and treatment of eating disorders.
  1  8    2.  As used in this section, unless the context otherwise
  1  9 requires:
  1 10    a.  "Diagnostic assessment of eating disorders" means
  1 11 medically necessary assessments, evaluations, or tests
  1 12 performed by a physician or psychiatrist licensed pursuant to
  1 13 chapter 148, a psychologist licensed pursuant to chapter 154B,
  1 14 an advanced registered nurse practitioner licensed pursuant to
  1 15 chapter 152 or 152E, a dietician licensed pursuant to chapter
  1 16 152A, a social worker licensed pursuant to chapter 154C, or
  1 17 a mental health counselor or marital and family therapist
  1 18 licensed pursuant to chapter 154D, to diagnose whether an
  1 19 individual has an eating disorder.
  1 20    b.  "Eating disorders" means pica, rumination disorder,
  1 21 avoidant or restrictive food intake disorder, anorexia nervosa,
  1 22 bulimia nervosa, binge eating disorder, other specified feeding
  1 23 or eating disorder, or any other eating disorder not otherwise
  1 24 specified.  The commissioner, by rule, shall define "eating
  1 25 disorders" consistent with definitions provided in the most
  1 26 recent edition of the American psychiatric association's
  1 27 diagnostic and statistical manual of mental disorders, as such
  1 28 definitions may be amended from time to time. The commissioner
  1 29 may adopt the definitions provided in such manual by reference.
  1 30    c.  "Pharmacy care" means medications prescribed by
  1 31 a licensed physician or psychiatrist and includes any
  1 32 health=related services deemed medically necessary to determine
  1 33 the need for or effectiveness of the medications prescribed,
  1 34 but only to the extent that coverage of such medications is
  1 35 included in the insured's health coverage benefits.
  2  1    d.  "Psychiatric care" or "psychological care" means
  2  2 direct or consultative services provided during inpatient
  2  3 hospitalization, partial hospitalization, residential
  2  4 care, intensive outpatient treatment, follow=up outpatient
  2  5 care, or counseling, provided by a licensed psychiatrist or
  2  6 psychologist.
  2  7    e.  "Therapeutic care" means medical care or behavioral
  2  8 interventions provided by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2  9 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 10 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 11 and family therapist.
  2 12    f.  "Treatment of eating disorders" means treatment that
  2 13 is identified in a treatment plan and includes medically
  2 14 necessary pharmacy care, psychiatric or psychological
  2 15 care, or therapeutic care, that is provided by a licensed
  2 16 physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced registered
  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.

  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:
  4 11    a.  Individual or group accident and sickness insurance
  4 12 providing coverage on an expense=incurred basis.
  4 13    b.  An individual or group hospital or medical service
  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.
       SF 2204 (2) 86
       av/rj/jh
  1 10    a.  "Diagnostic assessment of eating disorders" means
  1 11 medically necessary assessments, evaluations, or tests
  1 12 performed by a physician or psychiatrist licensed pursuant to
  1 13 chapter 148, a psychologist licensed pursuant to chapter 154B,
  1 14 an advanced registered nurse practitioner licensed pursuant to
  1 15 chapter 152 or 152E, a dietician licensed pursuant to chapter
  1 16 152A, a social worker licensed pursuant to chapter 154C, or
  1 17 a mental health counselor or marital and family therapist
  1 18 licensed pursuant to chapter 154D, to diagnose whether an
  1 19 individual has an eating disorder.
  1 20    b.  "Eating disorders" means pica, rumination disorder,
  1 21 avoidant or restrictive food intake disorder, anorexia nervosa,
  1 22 bulimia nervosa, binge eating disorder, other specified feeding
  1 23 or eating disorder, or any other eating disorder not otherwise
  1 24 specified.  The commissioner, by rule, shall define "eating
  1 25 disorders" consistent with definitions provided in the most
  1 26 recent edition of the American psychiatric association's
  1 27 diagnostic and statistical manual of mental disorders, as such
  1 28 definitions may be amended from time to time. The commissioner
  1 29 may adopt the definitions provided in such manual by reference.
  1 30    c.  "Pharmacy care" means medications prescribed by
  1 31 a licensed physician or psychiatrist and includes any
  1 32 health=related services deemed medically necessary to determine
  1 33 the need for or effectiveness of the medications prescribed,
  1 34 but only to the extent that coverage of such medications is
  1 35 included in the insured's health coverage benefits.
  2  1    d.  "Psychiatric care" or "psychological care" means
  2  2 direct or consultative services provided during inpatient
  2  3 hospitalization, partial hospitalization, residential
  2  4 care, intensive outpatient treatment, follow=up outpatient
  2  5 care, or counseling, provided by a licensed psychiatrist or
  2  6 psychologist.
  2  7    e.  "Therapeutic care" means medical care or behavioral
  2  8 interventions provided by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2  9 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 10 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 11 and family therapist.
  2 12    f.  "Treatment of eating disorders" means treatment that
  2 13 is identified in a treatment plan and includes medically
  2 14 necessary pharmacy care, psychiatric or psychological
  2 15 care, or therapeutic care, that is provided by a licensed
  2 16 physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced registered
  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical

  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.

  2 11 and family therapist.
  2 12    f.  "Treatment of eating disorders" means treatment that
  2 13 is identified in a treatment plan and includes medically
  2 14 necessary pharmacy care, psychiatric or psychological
  2 15 care, or therapeutic care, that is provided by a licensed
  2 16 physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced registered
  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:
  4 11    a.  Individual or group accident and sickness insurance
  4 12 providing coverage on an expense=incurred basis.
  4 13    b.  An individual or group hospital or medical service
  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.

  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.
       SF 2204 (2) 86
       av/rj/jh
  1 19 individual has an eating disorder.
  1 20    b.  "Eating disorders" means pica, rumination disorder,
  1 21 avoidant or restrictive food intake disorder, anorexia nervosa,
  1 22 bulimia nervosa, binge eating disorder, other specified feeding
  1 23 or eating disorder, or any other eating disorder not otherwise
  1 24 specified.  The commissioner, by rule, shall define "eating
  1 25 disorders" consistent with definitions provided in the most
  1 26 recent edition of the American psychiatric association's
  1 27 diagnostic and statistical manual of mental disorders, as such
  1 28 definitions may be amended from time to time. The commissioner
  1 29 may adopt the definitions provided in such manual by reference.
  1 30    c.  "Pharmacy care" means medications prescribed by
  1 31 a licensed physician or psychiatrist and includes any
  1 32 health=related services deemed medically necessary to determine
  1 33 the need for or effectiveness of the medications prescribed,
  1 34 but only to the extent that coverage of such medications is
  1 35 included in the insured's health coverage benefits.
  2  1    d.  "Psychiatric care" or "psychological care" means
  2  2 direct or consultative services provided during inpatient
  2  3 hospitalization, partial hospitalization, residential
  2  4 care, intensive outpatient treatment, follow=up outpatient
  2  5 care, or counseling, provided by a licensed psychiatrist or
  2  6 psychologist.
  2  7    e.  "Therapeutic care" means medical care or behavioral
  2  8 interventions provided by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2  9 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 10 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 11 and family therapist.
  2 12    f.  "Treatment of eating disorders" means treatment that
  2 13 is identified in a treatment plan and includes medically
  2 14 necessary pharmacy care, psychiatric or psychological
  2 15 care, or therapeutic care, that is provided by a licensed
  2 16 physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced registered
  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:

  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:
  4 11    a.  Individual or group accident and sickness insurance
  4 12 providing coverage on an expense=incurred basis.
  4 13    b.  An individual or group hospital or medical service
  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.
       SF 2204 (2) 86
       av/rj/jh
  1 24 specified.  The commissioner, by rule, shall define "eating
  1 25 disorders" consistent with definitions provided in the most
  1 26 recent edition of the American psychiatric association's
  1 27 diagnostic and statistical manual of mental disorders, as such
  1 28 definitions may be amended from time to time. The commissioner
  1 29 may adopt the definitions provided in such manual by reference.
  1 30    c.  "Pharmacy care" means medications prescribed by
  1 31 a licensed physician or psychiatrist and includes any
  1 32 health=related services deemed medically necessary to determine
  1 33 the need for or effectiveness of the medications prescribed,
  1 34 but only to the extent that coverage of such medications is
  1 35 included in the insured's health coverage benefits.
  2  1    d.  "Psychiatric care" or "psychological care" means
  2  2 direct or consultative services provided during inpatient
  2  3 hospitalization, partial hospitalization, residential
  2  4 care, intensive outpatient treatment, follow=up outpatient
  2  5 care, or counseling, provided by a licensed psychiatrist or
  2  6 psychologist.
  2  7    e.  "Therapeutic care" means medical care or behavioral
  2  8 interventions provided by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2  9 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 10 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 11 and family therapist.
  2 12    f.  "Treatment of eating disorders" means treatment that
  2 13 is identified in a treatment plan and includes medically
  2 14 necessary pharmacy care, psychiatric or psychological
  2 15 care, or therapeutic care, that is provided by a licensed
  2 16 physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced registered
  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.

  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:
  4 11    a.  Individual or group accident and sickness insurance
  4 12 providing coverage on an expense=incurred basis.
  4 13    b.  An individual or group hospital or medical service
  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.
       SF 2204 (2) 86
       av/rj/jh
  1 29 may adopt the definitions provided in such manual by reference.
  1 30    c.  "Pharmacy care" means medications prescribed by
  1 31 a licensed physician or psychiatrist and includes any
  1 32 health=related services deemed medically necessary to determine
  1 33 the need for or effectiveness of the medications prescribed,
  1 34 but only to the extent that coverage of such medications is
  1 35 included in the insured's health coverage benefits.
  2  1    d.  "Psychiatric care" or "psychological care" means
  2  2 direct or consultative services provided during inpatient
  2  3 hospitalization, partial hospitalization, residential
  2  4 care, intensive outpatient treatment, follow=up outpatient
  2  5 care, or counseling, provided by a licensed psychiatrist or
  2  6 psychologist.
  2  7    e.  "Therapeutic care" means medical care or behavioral
  2  8 interventions provided by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2  9 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 10 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 11 and family therapist.
  2 12    f.  "Treatment of eating disorders" means treatment that
  2 13 is identified in a treatment plan and includes medically
  2 14 necessary pharmacy care, psychiatric or psychological
  2 15 care, or therapeutic care, that is provided by a licensed
  2 16 physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced registered
  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.

  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical

  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.

  4 12 providing coverage on an expense=incurred basis.
  4 13    b.  An individual or group hospital or medical service
  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.
       SF 2204 (2) 86
       av/rj/jh
  2  5 care, or counseling, provided by a licensed psychiatrist or
  2  6 psychologist.
  2  7    e.  "Therapeutic care" means medical care or behavioral
  2  8 interventions provided by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2  9 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 10 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 11 and family therapist.
  2 12    f.  "Treatment of eating disorders" means treatment that
  2 13 is identified in a treatment plan and includes medically
  2 14 necessary pharmacy care, psychiatric or psychological
  2 15 care, or therapeutic care, that is provided by a licensed
  2 16 physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced registered
  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of

  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.
       SF 2204 (2) 86
       av/rj/jh
  2 11 and family therapist.
  2 12    f.  "Treatment of eating disorders" means treatment that
  2 13 is identified in a treatment plan and includes medically
  2 14 necessary pharmacy care, psychiatric or psychological
  2 15 care, or therapeutic care, that is provided by a licensed
  2 16 physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced registered
  2 17 nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental health
  2 18 counselor, or marital and family therapist.
  2 19    g.  "Treatment plan" means a plan for the treatment of  eating
  2 20 disorders developed by a licensed physician, psychiatrist,
  2 21 psychologist, advanced registered nurse practitioner,
  2 22 dietician, social worker, mental health counselor, or marital
  2 23 and family therapist that includes all of the following:
  2 24    (1)  A diagnosis.
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.

  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical

  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:

  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.

  4 21 employees.

  4 23 public health.

  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:
  4 11    a.  Individual or group accident and sickness insurance
  4 12 providing coverage on an expense=incurred basis.
  4 13    b.  An individual or group hospital or medical service
  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.
       SF 2204 (2) 86
       av/rj/jh
  2 25    (2)  Proposed treatment by type, frequency, and duration of
  2 26 treatment.
  2 27    (3)  Goals.
  2 28    (4)  All elements necessary for the third=party payment or
  2 29 prepayment of claims.
  2 30    3.  Coverage required by this section is limited to medically
  2 31 necessary diagnostic assessment and treatment of eating
  2 32 disorders in accordance with a treatment plan, that is provided
  2 33 by a licensed physician, psychiatrist, psychologist, advanced
  2 34 registered nurse practitioner, dietician, social worker, mental
  2 35 health counselor, or marital and family therapist acting
  3  1 pursuant to that person's applicable scope of practice.
  3  2    4.  Coverage required pursuant to this section shall be
  3  3 subject to copayment, deductible, and coinsurance provisions,
  3  4 and any other general exclusions or limitations of a policy,
  3  5 contract, or plan to the same extent as other health or medical
  3  6 services covered by the policy, contract, or plan.
  3  7    5.  This section shall not be construed to limit benefits
  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual

  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.
  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical

  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
  3 30    7.  The commissioner shall adopt rules pursuant to chapter
  3 31 17A to implement and administer this section.
  3 32    8.  This section shall not apply to accident=only,
  3 33 specified disease, short=term hospital or medical, hospital
  3 34 confinement indemnity, credit, dental, vision, Medicare
  3 35 supplement, long=term care, basic hospital and medical=surgical
  4  1 expense coverage as defined by the commissioner, disability
  4  2 income insurance coverage, coverage issued as a supplement
  4  3 to liability insurance, workers' compensation or similar
  4  4 insurance, or automobile medical payment insurance, or
  4  5 individual accident and sickness policies issued to individuals
  4  6 or to individual members of a member association.
  4  7    9.  This section applies to the following classes of
  4  8 third=party payment provider policies, contracts, or plans
  4  9 delivered, issued for delivery, continued, or renewed in this
  4 10 state on or after January 1, 2017:
  4 11    a.  Individual or group accident and sickness insurance
  4 12 providing coverage on an expense=incurred basis.
  4 13    b.  An individual or group hospital or medical service
  4 14 contract issued pursuant to chapter 509, 514, or 514A.
  4 15    c.  An individual or group health maintenance organization
  4 16 contract regulated under chapter 514B.
  4 17    d.  Any other entity engaged in the business of insurance,
  4 18 risk transfer, or risk retention, which is subject to the
  4 19 jurisdiction of the commissioner.
  4 20    e.  A plan established pursuant to chapter 509A for public
  4 21 employees.
  4 22    f.  An organized delivery system licensed by the director of
  4 23 public health.

  3  8 which are otherwise available to an individual under a policy,
  3  9 contract, or plan.
  3 10    6.  a.  Coverage of the diagnosis and treatment of eating
  3 11 disorders may be subject to other general exclusions and
  3 12 limitations of the policy, contract, or plan providing for
  3 13 third=party payment or prepayment of health or medical expenses
  3 14 not in conflict with the provisions of this section, such
  3 15 as coordination of benefits, and utilization of health care
  3 16 services, which include reviews of medical necessity and care
  3 17 management.

  3 18    b.  Medical necessity determinations and care management
  3 19 for the treatment of eating disorders shall do all of the
  3 20 following:
  3 21    (1)  Consider the overall medical and mental health needs of
  3 22 the individual diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 23    (2)  Not be based solely on the weight of the individual
  3 24 diagnosed with an eating disorder.
  3 25    (3)  Take into consideration the most recent practice
  3 26 guideline for the treatment of patients with eating disorders
  3 27 adopted by the American psychiatric association in addition to
  3 28 current standards based upon the medical literature generally
  3 29 recognized as authoritative in the medical community.
